          <div class="article__details--headline">
           <h1>
            <a data-ga-content-type="article" data-linktype="headline" href="https://www.cleveland.com/coronavirus/2021/03/ohio-records-931-new-coronavirus-cases-sunday-update.html">
             Ohio records 931 new coronavirus cases: Sunday update
            </a>
           </h1>
          </div>
          <div class="article__details">
           <div class="article__details--summary">
            The Ohio Department of Health reported Sunday that the number of confirmed or probable infections of the novel coronavirus had risen to 999,750, up ...
           </div>
           <div class="article__details--byline">
            <span>
             <span>
              Jane Morice
